American Company Requests Improvement of Hunan-Hubei Kung Fu Tea

Letter from Jinlong Foreign Firm to Hankou Municipal Commodity Inspection Bureau

The Jinlong Foreign Firm in this port previously sent a letter to the Hankou Municipal Commodity Inspection Bureau requesting improvements to Hunan-Hubei Kung Fu Tea. The translated text of the original letter is as follows: Dear Sirs, We recently received Mr. Winstan's report on the American survey of American opinions on Chinese tea. Much of it would be of interest to your bureau. Therefore, we are forwarding a summary.

Tea Chests

The materials used for Chinese tea chests are too weak. They are transported to America over long distances and cannot last. Damage often occurs. Such opinions have been repeatedly heard. After research by tea merchants in that country, it is generally believed that packing in Ceylon boxes made of three-ply plywood would eliminate these concerns. However, even if Ceylon boxes are used, America may not be willing to pay a higher price to purchase the tea. However, it would certainly be much easier to promote sales.

Competition

The competition from Japanese and Taiwanese tea is becoming increasingly fierce. Their greatest advantage is the sturdiness of their tea chests, which is far superior to that of Chinese Kung Fu Tea. Now, due to their clean and well-made tea, they have been granted special permission by the American government to be handled according to the Java standard tea method, that is, they can be used to blend Orange Pekoe and Pekoe. (Translator's note: Orange Pekoe and Pekoe are both types of black tea popular in Europe and America. If they can be blended, sales can be greatly increased.) However, Chinese tea is handled according to the Chinese Kung Fu Tea standard and cannot be blended into Orange Pekoe and Pekoe teas for sale. If it is to be blended, it must be specifically noted on the label. Although the standards for Japanese and Taiwanese black tea will be revised in the near future, the ban on using Chinese tea for blending may not be lifted. Several large American tea merchants have stated that Hunan-Hubei Kung Fu Tea is often cheaper than Japanese or Taiwanese black tea in terms of price. However, due to the restrictions of the aforementioned ban, they cannot use Kung Fu Tea to blend their brands. This is a pity. The following are opinions expressed by American tea merchants to Mr. Winstan: (A) One person said that they personally liked Kung Fu Tea, but for business reasons, they had to handle Japanese black tea, as the leaves of Japanese tea are cleaner and better suited to the market's taste. (B) One person said that they handled very little Kung Fu Tea, as Japanese and Taiwanese teas are very competitive in the market, and Japanese tea is particularly competitive. (C) One person said that they personally liked Kung Fu Tea, but as a blending tea merchant, they could not purchase Kung Fu Tea because of the aforementioned restrictions. (D) (A very large tea merchant, who is also a member of the American Tea Association) said that the business of standard Kung Fu Tea is small because it cannot compete with Japan and Taiwan. The above four opinions can represent the opinions of tea merchants across America. Our firm summarizes them further as follows: (1) The leaves of standard Kung Fu Tea must be selected more carefully in order to compete with Japanese tea. (2) There is very little hope of promoting precious black tea in America. What America needs is the cheapest tea. However, although the price of the tea is cheap, the quality cannot be too poor. It must meet the standard Kung Fu appearance set by the government. Therefore, attention must be paid to the cleanliness of the leaves, and the price must be similar to that of Japanese tea. (3) Tea chests must be improved. The worst Chinese tea chests are those from Xiangtan. For the sake of sturdiness, it seems possible to add four corner strips inside the box. (4) All tea chests must be lined with parchment paper between the lead lining (tin lining) and the tea leaves to prevent the tea from coming into contact with the lead. (This is a regulation of the American government and must be followed.) The above matters are related to your country's tea industry. It is said that your bureau is working hard to improve Chinese tea production. Therefore, we offer our views for your consideration.

Request to Dispatch Experts to Study Fire Well at Taizhou Guild Hall

Findings of Technician Zou's Investigation

Opinions Expressed by Various Parties

The fire well discovered in the Dingfeng Soap Factory within the Taizhou Guild Hall on Xinqiao Road, Lujiiawan, in southern Shanghai, has been previously investigated by personnel from the Municipal Social Bureau, as reported in previous newspapers. A Central News Agency reporter, believing that this matter is of great importance to industry, inquired with the Municipal Public Works Bureau. The bureau dispatched technician Zou Enyong to investigate and sent a letter to the Industrial Experiment Institute of the Academia Sinica and the Chinese Chemical Industry Association, requesting them to send experts to the bureau to conduct further research together. The findings of technician Zou's investigation are detailed below:

Fire Well Situation

The fire well is located in the Dingfeng Soap Factory within the Taizhou Guild Hall on Xinqiao Road in the southern Shanghai district. The well site used to be a water well, but it suddenly dried up. Although it was filled in, it repeatedly subsided, so it was filled with coal ash. Then it suddenly heated up, and flames poured out of the well pipe continuously. However, within a two-foot radius around the wellhead, there were also sporadic emissions of gas. Currently, the soap factory has built a brick wall around the well, with a large pot placed on top, filled with water, which is heated using the fire. The fire is extinguished at night and relit the next morning. This fire well has been discovered for more than a year. The gas in the well has been emitting constantly, seemingly without any increase or decrease.

Gas Testing

The gas was entrusted by the bureau to the Industrial Experiment Institute for detailed testing. The results are detailed in the table below. For reference, the qualities of natural gas invented by Luo Guorui and Shanghai Gas Company's coal gas are also listed in the table.

Gas Volume Measurement

The gas volume of the fire well was entrusted to the Shanghai Gas Company for measurement. The results are as follows: (1) The gas pressure fluctuates considerably, approximately equal to the height of a 5/8-inch water column. (2) Estimating with a 2-inch diameter well pipe, the gas volume is approximately 1,000 cubic feet per hour. (3) There is a lot of gas leakage. Based on this calculation, 24,000 cubic feet of gas can be produced per day. If leakage is prevented, the gas volume should be more than this.

Various Opinions

Since the discovery of the well, various parties have conducted investigations and expressed opinions, which are recorded below: (1) Shen Xiongqing, director of the Industrial Experiment Institute, believes that the production is not very large and will eventually extinguish itself. (2) Meng Enjun of the Shanghai Gas Company believes: A. Whether the source of this gas is sufficient is a problem. It is entirely possible that it will be extinguished. It is quite dangerous to invest in methods to utilize it. B. If the Dingfeng Soap Factory can add some equipment, the fire power can be increased. For example, according to the principle of a Bunsen burner, a hole can be drilled at a certain point below the pipe opening, so that air is mixed with the gas first, and then it is burned. Compared with the gas already ejected from the pipe opening, such as mixing with air, it will definitely get full oxidation, and the firepower will be greater. Currently, the outside of the iron pot at that place has a thick accumulation of black smoke, for this reason. C. There are more than one gas leakage around the well. If a surrounding wall and roof can be built to collect the gas volume in one place, the gas volume should increase. However, if the gas flows into this surrounding wall from the outside, it is feared that this surrounding wall will cut off the gas source. D. If a pump is used to extract the gas, it is quite feared that air or other miscellaneous gases will also be sucked in.

Yao Lifang, Manager of Yao Shuntai Fish Shop, Accused

Plaintiffs are Yao's Two Nephews

Accused of Uncle Embezzling Shop Funds

Yao Lifang, manager of the Yao Shuntai Fish Shop on Meibai Road, is accused of embezzlement and private enrichment, misappropriating more than 100,000 yuan from the shop's funds. He was recently sued in the First Special District Court by the shop owners, the Yao brothers, Yao Lindi and Yao Maodi, who hired lawyer Chen Tingrui to seek justice for his alleged crimes. Earlier, when the father of Lindi and others, Yuyuan, was alive, he initially started a fish business, working diligently and managing carefully. After several years of hard work, he had some savings. In the late Qing Dynasty during the Guangxu era, he invested in opening the Yao Shuntai Fish Shop at the northern end of the Xinzhapu Bridge. Because Lifang was a brother, he was given the position of weighing clerk. Lifang served diligently. In the third year of the Republic, Yuyuan suddenly suffered from a head wind disease and could not manage the shop's affairs. Because Lifang was a sibling and he seemed honest, he was appointed as manager, taking charge of all matters in the shop. In the fifth year of the Republic, Yuyuan was seriously ill and knew that he would not recover. Because his wife was a woman, his eldest son Lindi was only six years old, and his youngest son Maodi was still in swaddling clothes, he entrusted his orphans to Lifang on his sickbed, and instructed Lifang to carefully manage the shop's affairs, so that the business he created with his life's energy would not be ruined. However, after his brother's death, Lifang took advantage of the fact that his sister-in-law and nephews living in the shop were widows and orphans and could not do anything. He acted unilaterally and arbitrarily took private money from the shop to fill his greedy pockets, while only giving his sister-in-law and nephews 100 yuan each year for pocket money. He never announced the annual accounts to his sister-in-law. Yuyuan's wife was very dissatisfied, but because her two sons were still young and afraid of Lifang's power, she had to endure it for the time being. In recent years, Lindi and Maodi have grown up one after another. Although Lindi works in the shop, he only earns a salary of more than 10 yuan a month. He is not allowed to consult on the contents of the shop. Until last winter, Lifang felt that his two nephews were by his side and felt that he could not do what he wanted, so he took the initiative to take over, firing Lindi on the pretext and issuing an eviction order, ordering his mother and three children to move out of the shop. Lindi and others could no longer bear it and filed a criminal lawsuit against his uncle, saying that since their father's death, the defendant had intentionally embezzled the shop's funds. The total business volume of the shop each year is about 400,000 yuan. The commission taken by the shop is calculated at 7%, so that in addition to all expenses, the annual profit can be 10,000 yuan. For 20 years, all the annual profits have been swallowed by the defendant. Therefore, the defendant can live in luxury, successively taking three concubines, and purchasing 25 city houses and one residence on Gonghe New Road. He also built three city houses and a fishing pier in Beixinjing. The defendant was originally destitute. Although he was employed in the shop and received a salary, there was no private accumulation. The fact that he has such a huge amount of money must be entirely due to embezzlement. The facts are obvious. They requested that the defendant be punished according to Article 356 of the Criminal Code, and ordered to hand over the account books handled over the years for a thorough investigation of the actual amount of embezzlement, and another lawsuit will be filed. The trial was held by Judge Zhan Liangce in the afternoon of the previous day. First, the plaintiff stated the previous situation, and then the defendant Yao Lifang defended himself against the charges, vaguely saying that the fish shop opened by the plaintiff's father was declared bankrupt when he died. Today's fish shop was established by him. He retained the plaintiff's mother and three children in the shop out of brotherhood in order to fulfill his responsibility of education. The court then instructed the court to postpone the hearing and summon witnesses for another hearing.

Municipal Public Security Bureau Releases Crime Cases Within a Week

The Municipal Public Security Bureau released that 286 criminal cases occurred within the territory in the past week, including 68 theft cases, 48 rape and abduction cases, 45 injury cases, 43 opium cases, 8 red pill drug cases, 8 gambling cases, 13 robbery and robbery cases, 9 fraud cases, 3 homicide cases, 2 communist party cases, and 39 other criminal cases. Among them, theft cases were the most numerous. A total of 707 male and female criminals were arrested. All of them have been preliminarily examined by the Third Section and transferred to the District Court and other competent authorities for handling. The number of criminal cases discovered this week has decreased by six cases compared to last week, and the number of criminals discovered has decreased by 77 people compared to last week.

Jiang Kanghu Lectures on Temperance and Taciturnity

Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, Dr. Jiang Kanghu gave the third lecture on the Ten Precepts of Good Life at the Grand Auditorium of the YMCA in Baxianqiao. Dr. Jiang specially invited the Bingxun Stenography Society of Shanchangli, Kade Road, to record the lecture. There were more listeners than the first and second times. The upstairs and downstairs were almost full. The lecture was on the fifth and sixth precepts: temperance and taciturnity. The main points of the lecture are recorded below. Dr. Jiang lectured on temperance, saying that there are two kinds of desires: one is food, which is used to maintain life, and the other is sex, which is the sexual desire between men and women, which is used to continue life. Mencius said that food and sex are nature, and even Sakyamuni could not avoid these two things, but they must be restrained. There is no absolute thing in the world. For example, although arsenic is harmful, it can be used to replenish the body if used properly. Although ginseng is beneficial, it can sometimes kill people, so desires cannot be indulged. Dr. Jiang then lectured on taciturnity. He said that there are beneficial words and useless words. Chinese people use cursing their parents as a cliché. This kind of useless words should be less spoken, less until no speaking. Even beneficial words must be based on the person, the matter, the time, and the place before speaking. Otherwise, it is best to remain silent.

Great China Rubber Factory Held First Shareholders Meeting Yesterday

Re-electing the Second Board of Supervisors

The Great China Rubber Factory Co., Ltd. in this city held its first shareholders meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday at the Hong Kong Road Bank Club to report on last year's business situation and re-elect the second board of supervisors. The details are as follows:

Shareholders Present

There are more than 400 shareholders in the Great China Rubber Factory. Yesterday's attendees included Lin Kanghou, Yu Ziqing, Xue Fuji, Wu Zhesheng, Shi Weishan, Yu Xingben, Yang Weiyin, Huang Boqin, Xue Yangqing, and more than 300 others.

Xue's Report

After performing the necessary formalities, Chairman Yu Ziqing first delivered the opening speech, followed by manager Xue Fuji, who reported on the factory's business situation last year. He vaguely stated that since the factory was reorganized into a joint-stock company, it suffered from the impact of prolonged drought and social depression, resulting in no significant progress in business. According to the factory's largest lifeline, the production of overshoes accounted for the majority. Later, due to the intense competition from the same industry and the flooding of the market by a certain domestic product, which was sold at a low price, the large quantities of overshoes produced by the factory each month often suffered from excessive inventory and a gradual decline in sales. In order to find another way to earn a living, the factory colleagues spared no expense to send people abroad to purchase machines, carefully research, and manufacture automobile tires in order to recover profit rights. However, we are currently hoping that the government will provide strong protection so that the automobile tire products can be sold throughout the country, bringing glory to the country and honor to the nation. The former supervisors Shi Weishan, Lin Kanghou, and Yu Maotang then reported on the factory's assets and liabilities, respectively.

Re-election of Supervisors

After the report, the voting began. As a result, the elected supervisors were still the former members Lin Kanghou, Shi Weishan, and Yu Maotang. They took the oath of office on the spot. Finally, a dinner was held, and the meeting was adjourned until 9:00 PM in the evening.

Punishment for Seducing a Minor Girl

Zhang Genbao, a local resident living in a flat at No. 132 Puji Shilu, French Concession, works as a foreman in a construction factory. He has a daughter named Cuizhen, who is 16 years old this year. In the autumn of last year, she was seduced by Gu Amao (26 years old this year), a carpenter from Suzhou who lives next door, and committed adultery. The girl slept on the upper floor of her mother's room. Gu dared to go to Zhang's house to sleep with her. On the evening of December 6 last year, Gu went to Zhang's house again to continue their affair. Zhang returned home and heard the sound and discovered it. Just as he was about to go up to the upper floor to arrest him, Gu had already rushed down and fled home. Zhang immediately reported to the police station, and Gu was arrested. After questioning, it was learned that the girl voluntarily committed adultery, so no public prosecution was filed. Gu was only ordered to move out in three days. After Gu was released from the police station, he still did not move. The girl's father, Zhang Genbao, was unwilling to accept this and hired a lawyer to file a criminal lawsuit with the Second Special Court, accusing Gu of seducing a girl under the age of 15 and disrupting public morals. According to the lawsuit, the court opened a hearing presided over by Judge Li Changnian. Gu admitted to having intercourse with Zhang's daughter three times, voluntarily by the girl, and not induced. The girl did not admit to voluntarily inviting Gu to her home to commit adultery. The plaintiff requested that Gu be severely punished. The court ordered that the debate be concluded and the defendant be held for a scheduled sentence, which has been reported in previous newspapers. The previous day, the date of sentencing arrived, and the plaintiff and his daughter came to the court to await instructions. Judge Li came to the fourth criminal court and ordered the defendant to be brought to court. The judgment was that Gu Amao continuously raped a girl under the age of 16, and sentenced to one year and nine months of imprisonment. He also explained the meaning of the judgment to Gu, saying that in law, raping a girl under the age of 16 should be sentenced to more than seven years of imprisonment. Now, after questioning, it was learned that the girl volunteered, and you did not force it, which is excusable, so the sentence is reduced by two grades to one year and nine months. Gu replied obediently and was taken away by the bailiffs and returned to the detention center to await the appeal period before being sent to prison for execution.

Hooligans Violently Beat a Person to Death

Principal Culprit Xiao Zifan Fled, the Murderer Zhang Xiaomao was Arrested

Recommendation Shop was Afraid of Causing Trouble and Moved the Body into the Alley to Shirk Responsibility

Ni Lin's, a woman from Hefei, Anhui, is 45 years old this year. She is currently working as a maid at the home of Chen Li's, a Fujianese, at No. 14 Ming Deli, Xiafei Road, French Concession. Recently, she took a leave of absence and stayed in a house rented by fellow villagers at No. 137 Pushi Road. At 8:00 PM on the 1st of this month, Ni Lin's was pouring dirty water in front of the door, which splashed on a local rogue nicknamed Xiao Zifan who was passing by, which led to a verbal dispute. After being persuaded to disperse, Xiao Zifan was still not satisfied and immediately went to Zheng Yuanli, Beidiaolu, to gather Zhang Xiaomao (13 years old), a Jiangbei Haimen native who watched the alley in the area, and dragged Ni Lin's out to hold her down. The two men then committed the crime of beating her, causing Lin's to be unable to resist. She was punched and kicked and fell, injuring her head, and bleeding profusely. It was not until passers-by and neighbors persuaded them to stop. Later, Lin was injured and borrowed to lie down in Fang's recommendation shop at No. 53 Beidiaolu. Unexpectedly, due to excessive shock to the brain, she could not be treated in time and died at 7:00 AM the next morning. Fang Lin's, the owner of Fang's recommendation shop, was afraid of shifting the blame to herself and discussed with Luo Geng's, a fellow villager, and did not report to the police station. Instead, they took advantage of the early morning when there were few people and carried the corpse out and abandoned it in the neighboring Chunkuili alley at No. 55 to try to shirk their responsibility. Later, Xu Zhanghe (53 years old), a Shaoxing native who watched the alley in Chunkuili, discovered the corpse and reported it to the Lujiiawan French Police Station. After sending investigators to investigate, it was learned that the deceased had died from injuries from being beaten the night before. The murderer Zhang Xiaomao was arrested, Xiao Zifan had fled after hearing the news, and Fang Lin's (40 years old, Hefei native) and Luo Geng's (50 years old, also a Hefei native), the owners of the Fang's recommendation shop who moved the body, were brought to the case for investigation. At the same time, the body was sent to the coroner's office, waiting for the court to send someone to examine it today. The criminals Zhang Xiaomao and Fang Lin's, Luo Geng's, etc., were also sent to the court today for separate prosecution. The police station also sent a notice to all the detectives on duty to investigate and arrest the fleeing criminal Xiao Zifan and bring him to justice for interrogation.

Liu Zhengru's Concubine Sues for Paternity in Dongbao Case; Continued Trial

Dongbao Actually Denies Having This Biological Mother

Liu's Concubine Tearfully Pleads for Ye Shantao to Testify

Liu Zhengru (also known as Chengxu, Chengru), a wealthy merchant from Nanxun, passed away many years ago. During his lifetime, he extensively acquired concubines, resulting in a large number of children, totaling eighteen sons and daughters. His ninth son, Dongbao, was born to his fourth concubine, Yan Yuying. Dongbao is now over twenty years old. Yan was taken as a concubine by Liu in the first year of the Republic (1912). On the twenty-third day of the third month of the following year, she gave birth to Dongbao. However, the couple's abuse worsened daily, making it unbearable for Yan. Consequently, she was forced to leave the Liu family in the winter of that year. For over twenty years, she has wandered without support. Now that her son has come of age, he should

support his elderly mother.

She negotiated with Dongbao, but Dongbao actually denied being born to Yan. She had no choice but to hire lawyers Zhang Shizhao and Peng Yuanxun to file a confirmation lawsuit with the First Special District Court. This was reported in previous newspapers. Recently, Judge Yu Changzi held a continued trial. The defendant did not appear. The lawyers presented the separation agreement signed by Yan and the court settlement record from a previous lawsuit, stating that neither of these documents

mentioned Dongbao

as the plaintiff's biological son. Moreover, at the time of the settlement, the plaintiff was given eight thousand yuan. Now she is suing again, which is a case of double jeopardy and contrary to legal procedure, requesting that it be dismissed. The plaintiff, Yan Yuying, stated that she married Liu Zhengru as a concubine in the first year of the Republic and gave birth to Dongbao in the third month of the following year. The first wife was unusually abusive, and it became even worse at this time. She would always find ways to take away the milk purchased for Dongbao. There were countless insidious methods, too many to list. In the sixth month of that year,

I became pregnant again.

However, by August, the abuse had become unbearable. I left Liu in Qingdao and went alone to Tianjin. Liu then persuaded Ye Shantao to go north and persuade me to return to Shanghai on the seventh day of the eleventh month. However, because I was not tolerated by the first wife, I was refused entry into the house. Liu also refused to provide another residence. I had no choice but to follow Ye Shantao's advice and sign a separation agreement. At that time, Ye also said that Liu was old and that after his death, Dongbao would naturally still recognize me as his biological mother. Therefore, the agreement did not state that Dongbao was my biological son. The Liu family also believed that because

I was about to be divorced,

and the child in my womb was not yet fully developed, they found an abortionist to force me to abort the fetus before I could leave. My marriage to Liu as a concubine was originally arranged by Ye Shantao, and the separation was also mediated by Ye. Although Liu has passed away, Ye is still alive and can be summoned to testify. While speaking, tears fell like pearls, and she was extremely saddened. Subsequently, the lawyers for both parties debated the procedural point and concluded the debate. The judge announced that the verdict would be announced at a later date.

Chengdezhou Lightship Moves Position on Wuhu to Anqing Section of Yangtze River

The position of the lower section lightship at Chengdezhou on the Wuhu to Anqing section of the Yangtze River has now been moved. Its new position is one hundred and fifty-one degrees true north from the upper light bridge at the Tutou Bridge, at a distance of 1.2 nautical miles, i.e., east longitude 117 degrees 44 minutes, north latitude approximately 30 degrees 59 minutes. The Hydrographic Office has issued a notice to ships to this effect to alert the navigation community.

Publication of the National Studies Masterpiece "Introduction to National Studies"

Highly Respected by Contemporary Scholars

The term "National Studies" is interpreted slightly differently by people today, but generally, it refers to the achievements of our Chinese nation's cultural activities. If we want to improve the present and create the future, we must understand the past in all its aspects, and then innovate and modify it, building on the existing foundation to achieve greater excellence. This is a consensus among scholars, and writings such as "Introduction to National Studies" are also urgently needed at present. Now, Mr. Hu Huaichen, based on his usual research findings, has written "Introduction to National Studies," a book that provides a correct and concise account of the interpretation of National Studies, the purpose of studying National Studies, and the methods of studying National Studies. Many contemporary scholars have praised it. Chen Zaizun, a professor at Jiaotong University, said, "It can enable readers to gain novel common knowledge of National Studies in one day." Guo Butao, a professor at Fudan University, said, "This book has two characteristics: the emphasis on seeking knowledge and applying it to practical use makes the purpose correct. Although the classification still uses the old method, the argument in each chapter can actually integrate the past and the present, and distinguish and reconcile the right and wrong in a proper manner, so the understanding is sufficient." Zheng Shixu, a professor at Jiaotong University, said, "It is practical and applicable and can represent the author's reading vision and writing skills." Jiang Kanghu said that it can be "regarded as equally important as Zhang Zhidong's 'Qianxuan Yu'," and so on. This book has already been published and is distributed by Lehua Bookstore on Simalu in this city.

Social Affairs Bureau Approves New Pharmaceutical Industry Association's Industry Regulations

The industry regulations formulated by the Shanghai New Pharmaceutical Industry Association were submitted to the Social Affairs Bureau for registration and were approved yesterday. The regulations will be forwarded to the Public Security Bureau and the Court for reference. The original text of the industry regulations is transcribed below. Chapter 1, Article 1: These industry regulations are formulated by the Shanghai New Pharmaceutical Industry Association. Article 2: The purpose of these industry regulations is to maintain and promote the common welfare of the industry and to correct the malpractice of business operations. Article 3: All businesses engaged in new pharmaceuticals in the Shanghai area, whether members or non-members (including individual operators), must abide by these regulations. Chapter 2, Prices, Article 4: Industry prices. For all fast-selling goods, the price list shall be determined at any time by the Evaluation Committee organized by the Association, submitted to the Social Affairs Bureau for approval, and sent to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for record before being announced to all industries for compliance. What are fast-selling goods? Except when the producer requests it himself, the Evaluation Committee will determine it. The regulations of the Evaluation Committee shall be formulated separately. Chapter 3, Business, Article 5: Any person engaged in the new drug business within the city area must comply with the following provisions: (A) They must comply with the provisions of the Rules for the Management of Drug Dealers and the Rules for the Management of Medical Equipment Dealers, and submit them directly to the Municipal Health Bureau for registration and obtain a license. (B) Industries must use the weights and measures specified in the city. (C) If there is an exclusive sales contract among industries, the terms of the contract should be clearly stated and presented, and all industries should be invited to participate on their own, to show openness. Exclusive agents are not subject to this restriction. Article 6: When the industry holds a sale, all fast-selling goods must comply with the prices of fast-selling goods set by the Evaluation Committee, and no gifts are allowed. Chapter 4, Penalties, Article 7: If any industry violates the provisions of these industry regulations and is reported and the investigation is verified, the meeting shall submit the penalty and sanctions measures to the Social Affairs Bureau for review and execution. Chapter 5, Supplementary Provisions, Article 8: These industry regulations shall be implemented from the date of approval by the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs. Article 9: If there are factual obstacles to these industry regulations, the Association may submit a request for modification, or the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau may order the modification.

Publishing Circles

Insurance Yearbook to be Published Soon Our country's insurance industry has never had accurate statistics, which has caused it to remain at its inherent level and not increase. To seek the development of the business, it is necessary to first base it on historical facts. If there are no accurate statistics to show the truth of the facts, how can a path to progress be obtained? The editorial department of the China Insurance Yearbook, in view of this, compiled the 1935 Insurance Yearbook. The investigation and editing took six months to complete. It records the actual data obtained in a relatively systematic manner. The entire book is divided into four sections: the upper section is an overview of the insurance industry, which indicates the evolution, categories, and effects of the insurance industry; the middle section is an overview of the insurance industry in various countries around the world, which describes in detail the path of development of the insurance business in various countries; the lower section is an overview of the insurance industry in China, including a general overview of national insurance companies, which publishes the content of each insurance company, a survey of insurance business in various places, a report on the situation of the insurance industry in Guangdong, and various numerical statistics, which show the truth of the insurance business; the appendix is insurance laws and regulations and others, including government laws and regulations, translations of insurance policy contracts, and industry regulations and company charters. Anyone engaged in the insurance business must be prepared, and those who study the insurance business must read it. The entire book is printed on 23k Daolin paper, with a hardcover binding, in one large volume. The price is five yuan in national currency per copy, and the pre-order price is three yuan in national currency. The pre-order period for this city is extended for seven days, and the pre-order period for other cities ends on March 15.

Special Feature: Discussion on Sino-Japanese Economic Cooperation

— Mu Ouchu

Recently, Japanese newspapers have been widely reporting on Sino-Japanese economic cooperation. We believe that given the past animosity between China and Japan, to speak of cooperation so suddenly is far from reality. Although adjustment is a prelude to cooperation, we generally feel that given the current Sino-Japanese relationship, it is more appropriate to speak of adjustment rather than cooperation.

Regarding the so-called Sino-Japanese economic adjustment, according to the results of the discussion held by the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the 14th of February on economic adjustment toward China:

(1) To foster greater harmony between economic organizations and industrialists of both China and Japan, encouragement will be given to dispatching economic survey missions to China. However, this matter must be implemented after consultation with those involved in civil affairs.

(2) To thoroughly reform China's economy and finance to achieve self-reliance, Japan intends to provide the following types of assistance to China:

(A) China, as an agricultural country, is importing rice, wheat, and other food products from overseas, which is most unnatural. Japan is willing to provide China with economic and technical assistance in the agricultural sector.

(B) Cotton and other industrial raw materials that Japan must import from foreign countries will be encouraged for mass production in China, forming the foundation for Sino-Japanese economic adjustment, while also seeking to increase the purchasing power of Chinese farmers.

(C) To achieve rational management of Chinese industries, Japan is willing to provide China with economic and technical assistance when necessary.

(D) Implement a quota system for Sino-Japanese trade to increase the import of goods from both countries.

(3) Regarding the issue of Chinese silver outflow, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has consulted with the Ministry of Finance and the Yokohama Specie Bank, hoping that an international agreement can be established to alleviate the United States' silver purchase policy and the 1933 International Silver Agreement. However, concrete countermeasures have not yet been studied. Foreign banks, due to special relationships, mainly export silver from Shanghai, which has a significant impact. Japan hopes that China will improve its currency system, reorganize and unify bank notes, to reverse the precarious situation.

(4) The Japanese government is willing to establish a special bank in Shanghai with a capital of approximately 200 million Japanese yen to relieve the poverty of China's financial and industrial circles. This 200 million yen credit institution can not only facilitate the financial turnover of Sino-Japanese trade relations, but also bring great benefits to both countries. In particular, China's tariff revenue can be increased by this, and other policies can be improved smoothly.

(5) However, there is an absolutely necessary condition, which is to require China to strictly prohibit anti-Japanese activities, especially to thoroughly ban anti-Japanese education. It must be known that rejecting inexpensive and high-quality Japanese goods is the biggest obstacle to China's economic revival.

(6) China must reflect on tariffs, and not only refrain from raising them in the future but also specifically reduce them for Japan.

These are the official opinions of Japan. As for the economic circles, such as the Tokyo and Osaka Chambers of Commerce and Industry and other economic organizations, there have been discussions and expressions of Sino-Japanese economic cooperation, which are roughly similar to the above-mentioned guidelines of the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs and will not be quoted in detail here. However, what is worth our attention is why Japan is advocating Sino-Japanese economic cooperation at this time? We can explain this by considering (1) the widespread rejection of Japanese goods in the past year or two, and (2) the importance of the Chinese market to the Japanese economy.

The survival of the entire Japanese economy is entirely built on export trade. If various countries reject Japanese goods and the Chinese market cannot be arbitrarily used by Japan, then the Japanese economy will inevitably fall into collapse. However, the so-called economic nationalism is practiced by almost all countries in the world, and Japanese goods have no room to operate during the prevalence of this economic nationalism. The means by which various countries reject Japanese goods include raising tariffs, managing exchange rates, restricting imports, implementing import quota systems, and even severely prohibiting the import of Japanese goods and levying anti-dumping duties on Japanese goods, thereby preventing Japanese goods and protecting the development of their own industries. The situation of various countries rejecting Japanese goods is briefly described as follows:

United Kingdom: Raise tariffs to prevent imports.

France: Imposes high tax rates and exchange rate taxes to make it unprofitable for Japanese merchants; implements import quota systems for several important commodities such as ferromagnetic materials, timber, and aquatic products, to ensure that Japanese goods cannot freely enter French territory.

Germany: Roughly the same as France.

Italy: Raises tariff rates and manages exchange rates to ensure that Japanese goods entering Italy cannot make substantial profits.

Belgium: Implements an import quota system.

Switzerland: Implements an import quota system and bans the import of several commodities such as rubber shoes and cotton fabrics without government permission.

Netherlands: Same as Switzerland.

Austria: Implements raising tariffs, managing exchange rates, and deciding that Japanese goods cannot be imported without permission.

Hungary: Same as Austria.

Czechoslovakia: In addition to managing exchange rates, Japanese goods cannot be imported without permission.

Romania: Implements controlled imports for 130 types of goods and manages exchange rates.

Poland: Implements an import quota system.

Spain: Implements an import quota system and manages exchange rates.

Greece: Implements an import quota system, manages exchange rates, and exchanges Japanese goods for goods that are beneficial to itself.

Turkey: Implements an import quota system and manages exchange rates.

British India: In addition to raising tariffs, it also promulgated the Industrial Protection Act, abolished the Indo-Japanese Commercial Treaty, and entered into a reciprocal treaty with the United Kingdom to resist Japanese goods.

Malay Archipelago: Raises tariffs and establishes a special relationship with the United Kingdom to restrict the import of Japanese goods.

Dutch East Indies: Raises tariffs on general commodities, prohibits the import of rice and soybeans, and implements import quota systems for cement and cotton cloth, and issues emergency import restriction orders.

Philippines: Raises tariffs and abolishes ad valorem taxes.

Siam: Raises tariffs.

United States: In addition to raising tariffs, it levies anti-dumping duties on Japanese goods and prohibits the import of Japanese sake and beer.

Canada: Raises tariffs and implements exchange rate surtaxes.

Brazil: Raises tariffs and manages exchange rates.

Argentina: Manages exchange rates.

Chile: Uniformly raises tariffs by 50% and manages exchange rates.

Egypt: Raises tariffs.

Union of South Africa: In addition to raising tariffs, it levies anti-dumping duties.

East Africa: Raises tariffs.

British Africa: Declares secession from the Anglo-Japanese Commercial Treaty.

Australia: Manages exchange rates and levies exchange rate surtaxes.

Ecuador: Prohibits the import of Japanese raw silk and cotton cloth.

The widespread rejection of Japanese goods around the world is not because Japan forcibly occupied our Northeast provinces and withdrew from the League of Nations, thereby upholding justice, but because various countries cannot compete with Japanese goods that have low wages, low exchange rates, and lower costs. It is a natural result that various countries have to reject Japanese goods to protect their own industries. (To be continued)

Spring and Autumn

Tidbits

— (Wang Xiaolin)

Some people like to eat sparerib noodle soup, and others love beef fried rice, but I like to eat "cold shoulder." Although this dish is pitifully cold, it is also refreshingly cold. Compared to "eating cold rice at the table" and "drinking hot soup under the door," it is ultimately superior.

Miserly people, in love, will bring out money that they are reluctant to part with, either sadly or surprisingly generously. This fact is readily available around us. It seems that "love" is a wonderful remedy for "miserliness." Speaking from an economic standpoint, "love" should be the enemy of "money."

The new Eight-legged Essay has a few sentences that say: "Let the past be the past, and there is no need to yearn for the future. Reality is active before our eyes, seize this reality!" What exactly is reality? How to grasp this reality? "Drink today's wine today," "Monk of the day, strike the bell of the day." Is this what is meant by seizing reality?

Shepherd's Purse Song of the Third Day of the Third Month

— Zhen Lü

"On the third day of the third month, the weather is new, many beautiful women on the streets of Chang'an..." This Tang Dynasty poem, the record is actually like the current Gregorian calendar, wonderful! The third day of the third month was formerly the Shangsi Festival, which is exactly the time when spring is rippling. Investigating the normal state of physiological function, there will inevitably be women cherishing spring, so there are many beautiful women on the road! Who says that the works of our country's old poets are not scientific?

I remember a folk song, which also depicts the feelings and demeanor of girls in this season, while also portraying陋俗, both incisively and humorously; here is the entire song, accompanied by an explanation.

"Third day of the third month, shepherd's purse blossoms and forms peonies. Peony sister wants to marry. Pomegranate sister is the matchmaker. When the matchmaker arrives, the ghosts discuss. When the sedan chair arrives, the parents cry. Long towel, short towel, wipe away tears and then withdraw!"

Shepherd's purse is used as an object to indicate the season, and symbolizes a group of rural girls. The saying goes, "A young girl changes eighteen times"; shepherd's purse blooming can form peonies, metaphorically rural girls in their youth development stage, like flower buds just opening, will become beautiful. The time of the third day of the third month, with drums and flutes in every house, is exactly the weather for getting married; Peony sister is the same as others, pities her jade appearance, naturally wants to marry. Pomegranate sister, not yet in time physiologically, but also seduced by the annoying spring colors, then holds the idea of "walking in the spring breeze with summer rain," like adopting a daughter-in-law, and takes on the role of matchmaker. The matchmaker has ten unpardonable faults that are even worse; the bride also has many hypocritical solutions to imitate and force to be real. However, daughters are inevitable in human feelings, the sad feelings of leaving relatives have become the rhythm of crying when getting into the sedan chair, forced by vulgar rituals; this kind of tears shed for parents in name, is only a formality, rarely out of grief! The long and short towels wipe away tears and then withdraw, it can be seen that she is anxious and flustered, this is the true emotion revealed!

The composition of this song has a very ancient style, and it is particularly smooth and pleasant to sing, which is also worthy of praise.

Mass Grave

— Hu Chenzhou

"Look, this is the mass grave!"

Following the direction pointed by the boatman, I saw a building that was not much different from a dirt fortress, covered with countless mosses and wild vines. These creeping plants could not hide its broken walls and ruins, which seemed like the remains or relics of war. In the center of the front was a large opening, which seemed so deep that it was impossible to measure its depth. It stood alone in the twilight wilderness, surrounded by rugged ground and lush weeds stretching to the distant horizon.

Looking, looking, still not understanding the old boatman's strange term, I couldn't help but think and asked him, "What do you mean by mass grave? What is a mass grave?"

"Mass grave?" He stopped rowing and began to smile slightly. Obviously, he was proud of his familiarity with the ancient allusion. "You, sir, are not from here, so naturally you wouldn't know. But, ah, let me tell you! That is a pit, a pit for dead people!"

"A pit for piling up dead people, you say?" I couldn't help but shout.

"Yes, a pit for piling up dead people. There are corpses of children piled up inside, thousands upon thousands of them. You know, when poor families have children die, they don't have money to buy coffins, so they wrap the corpses of children in a rotten rush mat or a piece of rag, take them here, and throw them into that opening and it's done."

I was a little surprised. However, the boatman's indifferent expression in narrating this event immediately convinced me. The question knocked on my lips and returned to my throat again! I stared blankly at the terrifying repository of death, imagining the scene inside: there must be a special breath there, and countless microbes must be crawling. Some of the corpses there should have turned into skeletons long ago, some should have rotted, and some should be rotting, after rain, sun, and weathering!...

Suddenly I thought of those children lying under the white marble in the Shanghai Cemetery, one or two years old, or even only one or two months old. Their tombstones are exquisitely decorated with white marble goddesses of peace, white marble monuments engraved with the dates of birth and death of the deceased, and flowers in large glass domes, I was lost!

Go to the Countryside

A Study of World Famous Wines (Part 2)

— Zhao Yu

The Relationship Between Humanity and Wine: Northern peoples prefer to drink strong wines, while tropical peoples prefer to drink sweet and mild wines. Mongols in the frigid cold prefer to drink milk wine containing a small amount of alcohol. This is in terms of national character and climate. Milk wine is a by-product of the pastoral era, and grain wine is a by-product of the agricultural era. Wine originated in the wild era of mankind. (This is not intended as a joke by the author. In Europe, there is also this myth that at that time, wandering in the mountains and fields, picking tree fruits and grass fruits to fill their hunger, there was a demihuman wine god who taught the method of winemaking.) This is in terms of the era of wine's birth. The Chinese use rice, wheat, and sorghum to make wine, the Russians use rye, barley, naked barley, and corn to make wine, the Indians use coconut, and the Mexicans use agave. This is in terms of the raw materials being subject to natural control. People in cold regions say that wine can overcome the cold, and people in tropical regions say that wine can conquer the heat. This is in terms of the nation's view of wine. The color of wine also varies with the national character of different regions. Generally, peoples with a shorter evolution tend to like deep and strong colors, while the opposite is true for pale and light colors. Therefore, by observing their preferences, one can know what kind of people they are.

Entered the Gates of Hell

— (Xiaoxiao)

Some people say:

Losing "love" is like plucking out the heart.

Losing "affection" is like hooking away the soul.

The youth's common saying: "Love can irrigate youth"

Then; losing love is not: "Entering the Gates of Hell!"

Whereabouts

Impressions of Dali

— Jing'an

The name of Dali. Few people know it, but when the three words "Dali Stone" are mentioned, everyone knows it. This Dali is the place that produces Dali Stone, in the northwest of Yunnan, is the capital of the Nanzhao Kingdom in the Tang Dynasty and the Dali Kingdom in the Song Dynasty; the climate is mild, spring all year round, the territory is mountainous, the scenery is excellent! The four scenes of wind, flower, snow, and moon are very famous, that is, the flowers of Shangguan, the wind of Xiaguan, the snow of Cangshan, and the moon of Erhai.

Fifty miles west of Dali City, there is Cangshan Mountain, also known as Lingjiu Mountain, which is said to be the place where Guanshiyin Bodhisattva practiced Taoism. The mountain range originates from the southern branch of Kunlun Mountain, with nineteen peaks, the highest reaching 14,000 feet, overlapping peaks and ridges, stretching for more than a hundred miles, dignified and majestic, with trees standing tall, verdant and lovely. Ordinary mountains "open the forest mist at sunrise"; this mountain is not the case, only opens up briefly in the morning, when the sun rises in the east, the entire mountain is covered by clouds and mist. Only in July and August, there are no clouds all day long, only white clouds horizontally between the mountains like a white belt, called "Jade Belt Clouds", which is the so-called scenic spot of "Jade Belt Locking Cangshan". These situations are all personally witnessed. It's really a miracle! In addition, there are many flying springs, hanging cliffs thousands of feet, pouring down, the sound is like a Hong Zhong, shocking the ears.

What's even more interesting is that there are many ice creams sold in the mountains. At first, I thought there was an ice-making factory in this remote county; but asking the locals, they didn't know what kind of ice-making factory it was. Further investigating where their ice came from, I learned that it was taken from the top of Cangshan Mountain in winter and stored in a shady and humid rock, and taken out in the hot summer and mixed with cane sugar for drinks. According to Cangshan, snow accumulates after the chrysanthemums, and begins to melt in early summer. The time for its accumulated snow is so long, so the snow stored by the locals for sale is a lot, and the price is also cheap.

East of the city, there is a freshwater lake that is 20 to 30 miles wide and 90 miles long, shaped like an ear, which, according to the locals, is the ancient Yeyu Lake. Because it is shaped like an ear, it is also called Erhai, the benefit of fish and shrimp is quite large, and it is especially useful for the irrigation of farmland. There are three islands, four continents, and nine curves, all of which are very suitable for building gardens and huts. Thirty miles south of the city, where the Erhai water descends, there is a stone bridge called "Tianqiao", the secluded gorge is deeply hidden, the stone bridge spans left and right, like a family; relying on nothing in the air, only crossing one person, the situation is dangerous! When I passed this bridge, I was shocked and wanted to turn back repeatedly! After crossing the bridge, walking a hundred paces west, there is a rock, in front of the rushing stream, splashing waves like plum blossoms; this bridge is also called "Buxie Meiqiao", I am afraid it is from this that it came. When the bright moon rises in the east in the evening, the waves sparkle, and the fishing boats sway, it is even more interesting. This is the night scene I saw on the day I went to Erhai, I don't know if the so-called "Erhai Moon" is such a scene?

Little Western Paradise

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 9: Being Poor at Complimenting, Begging People to Suffer Reprimands, Failing to Return Home, Being Confused by Exaggeration

Jia Duocai smiled lightly at him: "Thank you, Brother Zhang, for your good intentions to be a persuader for us, this wild horse doesn't have to run too far." Zhang Jiefu smiled and said: "That's fine too, I think this sister-in-law is an overly honest person, there's no need to speak to him evasively, just tell him everything in a few words, and let him make the decision." So he got up two steps, walked to Mrs. Hu's side, leaned down and said to him: "This Mr. Jia has long intended to take your daughter as a concubine, you know that. How much money do you want before you agree?" Mrs. Hu and his mother-in-law, as well as his family member Mrs. Hu, who wasn't hoping to get a sum of money from Yueying to relieve everyone's difficulties. As for how much money they could ask for, they really had no standard. Mrs. Hu's intention was that two generations of widows could live a lifetime following this girl, which would be fine. If there were a few coins in hand to spend, naturally it would be good. Even if there was no money, with such a son-in-law who runs a silver shop, what would they have to worry about? Moreover, they were afraid that the other party would not agree if they asked for too much, and they were afraid of being cheated if they asked for too little. Zhang Jiefu raised such a question to him, suddenly, how could he answer it, he babbled for a while, and finally managed to squeeze out two sentences, he smiled and said: "Mr. Jia is a living god of wealth, how could he give less? I don't know how to speak, what do you want me to say?" Zhang Jiefu turned his head and said: "Brother Jia, what do you mean?" Jia Duocai gave him a wink, fixed his eyes outside the room, and Zhang Jiefu followed him out. After about ten minutes, only Zhang Jiefu came in alone, pulled Mrs. Hu's sleeve, let him stand up, and then let Yueying lean against the wall with him. He whispered: "Sister-in-law, do you see those silver dollars on the table? If your heart is moved, those silver dollars will be yours immediately." This was another unprecedented miracle in Mrs. Hu's ears, how could there be such a strange thing, his heart was flustered, what should he agree to? He suspected that this was a dream. (147)

Records of Ephemeral Fragrance from the Imperial Court

— Original work by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

Speaking of myself, when I went, I was of course very happy, always thinking that this trip would be extremely rewarding, but little did I know that I only saw many strange lanterns and smelled the stench of lilacs, which was enough to make people sick for days and nights, how could it not make people disappointed and lose all their enthusiasm.

Suddenly, Li Lianying hurriedly walked from his own carriage to the Empress Dowager's carriage.

"Reporting to the Empress Dowager! In just a few minutes, the train will arrive in Tianjin!" He kowtowed and whispered his report, his face plastered with the usual obsequious and shameless smile. "It seems necessary to stop for a while so that those ministers can perform the briefest of ceremonies."

The Empress Dowager, however, was not listening to him today and replied very decisively:

"The train is not allowed to stop under any circumstances! There is only one compromise; that is, after our train enters the station, you should first keep a close watch, and when it is closest, you can report back to me!"

Before long, the outline of Tianjin gradually became visible; the Empress Dowager, knowing that Yuan Shikai and his officials would soon be kneeling on the platform to watch us pass by, became more attentive in her preparations. On the one hand, she tidied her own clothes, and on the other hand, she told us not to move around and to stand extra straight. At the same time, the driver had also received a hint and hurriedly reduced the speed of the train. In fact, given the Empress Dowager's status, such a deliberate slowing down of the train to receive their respect was already a great favor: however, the Empress Dowager did indeed attach special importance to Yuan Shikai, and she felt that simply slowing the train was not enough to repay his kindness, so she took a further step in expressing her appreciation. (258)

Sports News

Chairman Chiang's Telegram Order to Public Servants to Pay Attention to Physical Education

Nineteen out of ten public servants in various agencies indulge in ease and comfort

Supervising officers should be responsible for promoting and strictly supervising

Each person must choose a sport and practice it regularly

(Central News Agency, Hankou, 2nd) Chairman Chiang telegraphed an order on the 1st to all agencies to vigorously promote physical education, stating, "To all Pacification Commissioners, Commanders-in-Chief, Provincial Party Headquarters, Provincial Governments, and forwarded to the Education Department for consideration. It is found that sports are an important task to temper the national physique and build a strong race to save the country, and should be vigorously promoted and universally developed. Therefore, the two skills of archery and horsemanship in ancient China were listed in the six arts as compulsory subjects for scholars and officials. Today, the world's great powers, from top to bottom, and men, women, and children, all have a strong passion for sports and strive continuously. On the other hand, in our country in recent years, although there are many schools in various provinces and cities, they have gradually been able to pay attention to this, but the schools generally focus on the training of a small number of athletes, neglecting the cultivation of all students. As for public servants in various party, government, and military agencies, nineteen out of ten indulge in ease and comfort and have no interest in sports. Such a situation is contrary to the way to transform and build a healthy nation. Therefore, it is strictly ordered that all teachers and students above the middle school level, teachers of various elementary schools, and staff of various party, government, and military agencies must each choose a sport or recreational subject from now on. The responsible officers of each agency and the principals of each school shall be responsible for organizing, strictly supervising, and assigning instructors. Practice must be carried out regularly between 5:00 pm and 6:00 pm every day, and between 4:00 pm and 5:00 pm in winter, continuously and without interruption. In the event of windy, rainy, or snowy seasons, when outdoor exercise is inconvenient, the responsible officers and the Education Department should consult on remedial measures, so as to maintain consistency and avoid sporadic efforts. This is the only important point. It is hoped that the above instructions will be followed separately, and the party, government, military, and academic institutions of each province will jointly draft a law and implement it earnestly. All levels of agencies and schools in all localities under their jurisdiction should also abide by it. A report should be submitted for record, so that it can be inspected at any time, so as to make a judgment. Chiang Kai-shek, winter."

Jewish Tenacity Wins in a Hard-Fought Swimming Match

The result was three to two

The situation was extremely tense

The swimming match between Youyou and the Jewish team took place yesterday afternoon at 3:00 at the Shenyuan football field, as one scene of the Western League football A group match. Under the contest, the Jewish people fought desperately, and were able to create a stalemate situation. The competition was quite fierce. In the first half, Youyou led with a score of two to one. The final result was three to two, with Youyou winning.

Youyou launches a frontal attack

Youyou kicked off, taking the initiative. The Jewish team, relying on its inherent bravery, resisted vigorously, advancing and retreating, with uncertain risks. After a melee lasting for five minutes, Luo Haiguang dribbled deep, Chen Shikai shot fiercely, hitting the mark accurately. After a moment, Zhong Yongsheng crossed from the edge, and Sun Jinshun scored with one shot, but it was not counted because of offside. Youyou's momentum was not diminished by this. Zhong Yongsheng rose up from the edge, dribbled into the hinterland, and the two Jewish inside guards blocked the ball with their chests, causing a disaster and being penalized with a twelve-yard penalty. Sun Tieleg succeeded immediately, winning by two goals.

The Jewish team pulls back a goal

After losing two goals in a row, the entire Jewish army was filled with indignation and launched a punitive expedition. Pang Queke received the cooperation of the left and right inside forwards and regained a goal. Afterwards, Sun Jinshun had two excellent scoring opportunities, but both were brilliantly saved by the Jewish goalkeeper, which was a pity. Before long, the first half ended, with Youyou leading by two to one.

Each team scores two, resulting in a draw

In the second half, the Jewish team, with its indomitable spirit, launched a desperate counterattack on Youyou's hinterland. For a time, the situation was turbulent. Fortunately, the two inside guards joined forces to defend, avoiding disaster. The Jewish team repeatedly failed to score. The right inside guard, Hashek, had a loss of control in his movements and was sent off the field. From then on, the Jewish team faced the battle with ten men, and the counterattack became even more intense. Toutuo Man and Pang Queke advanced side by side. Wang Shusen and Jiang Shanjing could not stop them, and S. Greenburgh shot angrily, and because it was close, goalkeeper Zhang Rongcai could not save it, resulting in a draw of two goals each.

Youyou plays a triumphant song

With the tie established, the offensive of both sides became more tense. Sun Jinshun was indeed extraordinary, rushing straight in alone. At a considerable position, he kicked the ground, and the ball shot out like an arrow. The Jewish goalkeeper was caught off guard. This ball was kicked very cleanly and was a spectacle. The audience cheered wildly. At this point, the Jewish team's movements became more violent. S. Greenburgh was arrogant and uttered obscenities to the referee and was immediately sent off the field. After a long time, the time was up, and Youyou won against the Jewish team by three to two.

Youyou Team

Zhang Rongcai, Wang Shulin, Jiang Shanjing, Liang Shutang, Chen Zhenxiang, Yun Feng, Wang Nanzhen, Chen Shikai, Luo Haiguang, Sun Jinshun, Zhong Yongsheng

Jewish Team

Di Quli, G. Greenburgh, Hao Leisidan, Jie Kebu, M. Greenburgh, Hashek, L. Greenburgh, S. Greenburgh, Bei Lingai, Pang Queke, Toutuo Man

Junior High School Health Textbooks to Add Leprosy Content

The Ministry of Education approved the application of the China Leprosy Relief Association for special training orders to the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, stating that the China Leprosy Relief Association has requested to include leprosy facts in textbooks at all levels. American University Travel Group to Visit China for Investigation

Columbia University in the United States will organize a travel group to come to China, first to Shanghai, to investigate family education and economic education. They sent a letter in advance requesting facilitation. After consultation between the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Education, the group was notified to contact directly Li Zhao Huan, President of Shanghai Jiaotong University, and Liu Zhan En, President of Shanghai Jiangnan University, for a faster approach.

Meeting to Revise Standards of Weights and Measures

The Executive Yuan, due to the case of the Chinese Physical Society requesting to revise the names and definitions of the standard units of weights and measures, has separately ordered the Peiping Research Institute, the Central Research Institute, the Ministry of Education and Industry, the Ordnance Administration, the Chinese Physical Society, and the Chinese Engineering Society to each send one or two representatives to attend the meeting at the Executive Yuan on March 1 and 2. Except for the representative of the Peiping Research Institute, who did not make it in time, all the others attended. The two-day meeting was very successful. The drafts proposed by the Chinese Physical Society and the Ministry of Industry were reviewed and generally decided that the Executive Yuan will compile the results of the two-day meeting and review and then solicit opinions from various academic institutions and organizations, and hold another meeting in mid-May to make a final decision.

Jiangsu Education Department Telegrams to Investigate the Educational Administration Performance of Various Counties

Educational Committee Members of Nan Hui and Other Counties Reprimanded

Jiangpu Educational Committee Member Yu Jingbo Dismissed

Zhenjiang News, Since the Jiangsu Education Department implemented telegrams to investigate the performance of various county bureaus, it has been quite effective. The total number of investigations conducted this year up to February includes over a hundred pieces of performance information from Qidong, Songjiang, Nanhui, Taicang, Haimen, Wujiang, Yixing, Taixing, Huaiyin, Funing, Yancheng, Dongtai, Xinghua, Baoying, Fengxian, Jiangpu, and Yangzhong. Approximately thirty educational committee members from various counties had their inspection reports extracted, all of whom have been sent to the department on schedule for review and return. Detailed instructions and corrections have been added for points that need improvement. The reports of the educational committee members of Nanhui, Funing, and Taixing counties had discrepancies and were all reprimanded. Jiangpu educational committee member Yu Jingbo had a record of repeated reprimands by the Education Department for unsatisfactory work. The telegram investigation of inspection reports this time also failed to be submitted on time, and it was deemed difficult to improve, so he was dismissed. Due to the shortage of disasters in the county's education in the past, there are not many schools now. In order to save administrative expenses, the position of educational committee member will not be temporarily filled. All inspection matters will be the responsibility of the county school superintendent. In addition, the documents of the Jiangpu and Yangzhong county governments on handling the provincial school superintendent's inspection of the schools in each county and the instructions for rectification have also been telegrammed for review. All the ordered matters have been handled separately, showing a practical approach to rectifying local education.

National Shanghai College of Commerce New Campus Holds Groundbreaking Ceremony

The construction of the new campus of the National Shanghai College of Commerce, undertaken by the local Lu Genji Construction Company, has commenced. President Pei Fuheng of the college has spared no effort in supervising the construction, so the work has been progressing very quickly. Yesterday, a groundbreaking ceremony was specially invited, attended by Minister Lei Zhen from the Ministry of Education, Li Dachao from the Municipal Government, Jiang Jianbai from the Education Bureau, Wu Songgao from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Jin Tongyin and other representatives from industry and commerce and various schools, as well as more than 600 faculty, students, and alumni. The details are as follows:

Groundbreaking Ceremony of the National Shanghai College of Commerce

— Photo by Wang Kai

Meeting Affairs: On that day, the college temporarily decorated the meeting place, fully hanging Party and national flags and school flags. On both walls were congratulatory messages from the National Shanghai Medical College and the College's Alumni Association, which were very eye-catching.

Summary of Speeches: First, President Pei, as chairman, delivered a speech, stating briefly that after the college's campus was destroyed by artillery fire during the Shanghai War, it had experienced various difficulties. In recent years, thanks to the guidance of Minister of Education Wang and the efforts of all faculty and students, the college's affairs had returned to normal and progressed in an orderly manner. Now, it was the first to restore the campus in the war zone, so holding the groundbreaking ceremony today was deeply commemorative. In the future, it will further expand the campus to become the only perfect institution of higher learning for commercial studies. He hoped that the Ministry of Education and all sectors would continue to provide assistance, and that faculty and students would become more motivated to cultivate talented and skilled commercial talents, to modernize Chinese commerce, strive for economic construction, and complete the college's mission, which would be very fortunate. Finally, he thanked the guests for attending the ceremony. Minister Lei Zhen, representing Minister of Education Wang, then gave a speech, stating the general idea that, the College of Commerce is located in a major trading port and is also the only national commercial institution, and the government has high expectations. Therefore, even in a state of financial difficulty, it still allocated funds to build the campus. Today, at a time when Chinese commerce is depressed and the economy is declining, enrollment has increased sharply, and domestic products cannot be promoted in the international market. [sentence fragment due to damaged text], striving to revitalize commerce and modernize it, is the only way to compete with others, increase national wealth, and lay the foundation for the country. Everyone should take this to heart and pursue advanced studies, not to betray the government's intention to cultivate commercial talents. Mayor Wu's representative, Li Dachao, then gave a speech, briefly stating that the reconstruction of the College of Commerce campus not only shows the government's emphasis on commercial education, but also the result of President Pei's leadership of faculty and students. The Municipal Government expresses its deep pleasure and intends to provide assistance for its early completion. The construction plan for the Greater Shanghai Municipality is currently underway in various ways. After the completion of various cultural institutions in the urban area, it will provide the College of Commerce with many conveniences. It is hoped that everyone will bury their heads in hard work, hoping to contribute what they have learned to the country and the nation. Finally, Jiang Jianbai, representing the Education Bureau, gave a speech, stating that in recent years, the domestic atmosphere of studying has plummeted. The College of Commerce is uniquely able to reverse the decline and create a good academic atmosphere. Now that there is this new campus, there will certainly be more satisfactory results. It is hoped that the faculty and students of the College of Commerce will come out and transform the academic atmosphere, from near to far, and extend it to the whole country, one is to strive for the construction of culture, and the other is to fulfill its task of universally promoting culture, so the revival of the nation can be expected. After the speeches, the groundbreaking ceremony was held, photos were taken, and the meeting adjourned.

Awaiting the Establishment of the Central Preparatory Committee

To Be Submitted by the Ministry of Education to the Association for Review

The Municipal Children's Welfare Committee received instructions from the Municipal Government yesterday, stating: Approved is the Ministry of Education's letter No. 2269 of General Affairs No. 42 of the 24th year of the Republic, stating that the letter No. 3471 of your Municipal Government regarding the Shanghai Children's Welfare Committee's submission of the Chinese Children's Year Implementation Measures, together with the original, is respectfully requested to be jointly reviewed and adopted.
